                 E-8                                                                                         A+W Business Production
Production              E

                    Tutorial




             A+W Business
                 Tutorial                                                                                     Overview




                                       Overview
                                       The tutorial on the Production module deals with the basics of the transfer to
                                       production and shipping in A+W Business. It is based on and requires knowl-
                                       edge of master data.

                                           The functions depend on the enabled modules
                                           Please note that the individual functions are only available if the corre-
                                           sponding modules and interfaces have been installed and enabled.

                                           Should you detect functions in this documentation which are not available
                                           in your version, please contact A+W Software GmbH.

                                       Subjects
                                       The training on the Production module consists of the following subjects:
                                       •   Basic Ideas on Production and Dispatch
                                       •   Transfer to Production
                                       •   Reports from Production
                                       •   Logistics
                                       •   Overviews
                                       •   Additional Features

                                       Required knowledge
                                       The tutorial is meant for those who organize the shipping in A+W Business.
                                       Participants must be familiar with the master data concept and order entry in
                                       A+W Business.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 A+W Business Production                                                                           E-11
                 Overview                                                                                Tutorial




                            Documentation
                            The following documents are available on the Production module:

                            Handout                   Printout of tutorial for training session

                            PDF                       Complete documentation
                                                      • Tutorial
                                                      • Software reference
                                                      • Index

                            Online help <F1>          Context-sensitive dialog help for the A+W Business
                                                      software references and tutorials on the basic version


                            Tutorial Structure
                            This tutorial consists of subjects with several training modules each. Each
                            module consists of the following elements:

                            Overview                  Each training module starts with an overview of the
                                                      major topics:
                                                      • Objectives: What shall be conveyed?
                                                      • Benefit: What can this knowledge be used for?
                                                      • Maxims: Which correlations are to be remembered?

                            Concepts                  First, the concepts and terms of the corresponding
                                                      training module will be explained. This is followed by
                                                      examples and instructions.

                            Exercises                 There are exercises featuring special tasks for some of
                                                      the training sessions.

                            Cross-references          At the end of each training module there is a section
                                                      with cross references pointing out additional information
                                                      in the software reference and in other sections.
                                                      This will help you to extend your newly acquired
                                                      knowledge.


                            Reading instructions
                            The contents of a training module are based on the knowledge conveyed in
                            the previous module. We therefore recommend that you do not skip any mod-
                            ules.
                            If you are already familiar with a subject, you should at least read the summary
                            at the start of the module in order to bring the main details to mind.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-12                                                              A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                                       Overview




                                       Display Conventions
                                       Certain parts of sentences are specially marked. Their meanings are:

                                       Italics                  mark character strings defining elements of the
                                                                software, e.g. the Transfer to production dialog.

                                       Bold                     marks character strings to be entered via the keyboard,
                                                                e.g.: Enter the value 0.

                                       >                        The so-called breadcrumb trail shows how to open a
                                                                dialog, e. g. Production > Production > Transfer to
                                                                production.

                                       []                       Square brackets mark buttons in a dialog, e. g. [OK] to
                                                                save the data.

                                       <>                       Angle brackets refer to keys or shortcuts on the
                                                                keyboard, e. g. <F1> is used to open the online help.
5.20 / 04-2020

                                        This chapter provides a brief overview of the program sections that will be ad-

                 E-14                                                                      A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                                    Overview




                                       Rack management
                                       Use this section to manage own and external racks and to get an overiew of
                                       the current stock on hand.
                                        “Rack Management” on page E-157
                                        Software Reference, “Rack Management” on page E-252

                                       Schedule
                                       This section will give you an overview of dates and capacities.
                                        “Date Overview” on page E-115
                                        Software Reference, “Date Overview” on page E-266

                                       Customs management
                                       This section can be used to create customs lists for the export of goods.
                                        Software Reference, “Customs Management” on page E-281

                                       Optimization of quotations
                                       This is where you can transfer quotations to production to be optimized.
                                        “Transfer to Quotation Optimization” on page E-50
                                        Software Reference, “Optimization of Quotations” on page E-289

                                       Document data
                                       This is where you can view lists of orders and the corresponding purchase or-
                                       ders, and correct dates if necessary. This dialog is described in detail in the
                                       Sales tutorial.
                                        Sales, “Document Data” on page C-736

                                       Product info
                                       This section can be used to display information on the products defined in
                                       A+W Business. You can check the product structure, prices and availability.
                                       This dialog is described in detail in the Sales tutorial.
                                        Sales, “Product Information” on page C-600

                                       Fax message
                                       This section allows you to issue and dispatch fax messages to your customers
                                       and suppliers directly from A+W Business. This dialog is described in detail in
                                       the Overview tutorial.
                                        Einleitung, “Standard-Menüs” auf Seite A-53


                                       Additional information
                                        Einleitung, “Elemente des Programmfensters” auf Seite A-52
                                        Sales: Software Reference, “Document - header data” on page C-415

                 A+W Business Production                                                                          E-15
                 Basic Ideas on Production and Dispatch                                                                                           Tutorial




                                              Basic Ideas on Production
                                              and Dispatch
                                              Orders have been entered in document management, the items of which have
                                              to be produced. The orders and order items have to be transferred to produc-
                                              tion for this purpose. The data which are relevant for production are saved in
                                              a file which can be imported by the production software.
                                              By means of the ERP Webservice, these transfer files can be directly passed
                                              on to the production software A+W Production to be imported.


                        A+W Business                                                                      A+W Production
                                                                                 Report                (Production software)


                            Status
                            Order                           Transfer to Production               Production
                            • Item 1: Production                                                 • Item 1: Production
                            • Item 2: Production                                                 • Item 2: Production
                              and purchasing                                                       waiting for delivery
                            • Item 3: Purchasing with
                              direct delivery
                            • ...
                                                                                                     Report to production

                            • Item n



                                                                                 P.O.

                                  Deadline
                                 monitoring
                                                               Direct delivery




                                                                                    Receipt of
                                                                                     goods
                               Route planning



                                                                                                                            Legend:
                                 Shippping                          Customer                                                Production software


                 Fig. E-2       Transfer to production and dispatch organization


                                              This sketch shows you the interaction of the transfer of orders to Production,
                                              reports from Production, and the organization of dispatch.
                                              The order status controls the correct booking sequence so that an order can
                                              only be transferred to production if it has the appropriate status, for example.
                                              The current state of production is reported back to A+W Business. Based on
                                              this, the status of each order item is changed, and finally that of the entire or-
5.20 / 04-2020




                                              der. Depending on how a company is organized, the status is raised automat-
                                              ically or manually. The data including the change of status can be entered via
                                              barcodes, which helps to reduce input errors considerably.



                 E-16                                                                                                       A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                    Basic Ideas on Production and Dispatch




                                       Based on capacity checks, production and delivery dates can be examined
                                       and amended if necessary so that dispatch can be optimally organized.
                                       Route and loading lists are created for dispatch, allowing the vehicles to be
                                       loaded optimally based on route and the weight permitted.

                                       Procedures in production and dispatch
                                       The sequence of the individual actions for production and dispatch of an order
                                       depends on the conditions in your company.
                                       The process can be organized like this, for example:
                                       •   Transfer to Production
                                       •   Check report from Production
                                       •   Print delivery notes
                                       •   Route planning
                                       •   Print loading list and receipt acknowledgement list
                                       •   Shipment
5.20 / 04-2020




                 A+W Business Production                                                                        E-17
                 Transfer to Production                                                                         Tutorial




                                          Transfer to Production
                                          This session shows you how to transfer orders or quotations to Production.
                                          This includes the following training modules:
                                          •   “Transfer to Production – Variations” on page E-19
                                          •   “Transfer to Production without Capacity Planning” on page E-27
                                          •   “Transfer to Production by A+W Business Capacity Planning” on
                                              page E-41
                                          •   “Transfer to Production by A+W Production Capacity Planner” on
                                              page E-45
                                          •   “Transfer to Quotation Optimization” on page E-50
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-18                                                                      A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                        Transfer to Production




                                       Transfer to Production – Variations
                                       Order data are transferred to A+W Production or another production program
                                       when they have reached the defined minimum status. The data can be trans-
                                       ferred in the following ways:
                                       •   Without capacity planning:
                                           The orders are directly transferred to Production without entering them in
                                           capacity planning first.
                                       •   With A+W Business Capacity Planning
                                       •   With A+W Production Capacity Planner
                                           In the last two cases, the orders will pass through the following steps:
                                           – First, the orders are transferred to capacity planning.
                                           – The status of the order is raised after the production and delivery dates
                                             have been confirmed or amended.
                                           – Machine capacities are reserved now.
                                           – After that, the orders are transferred to production and can be produced.
                                       The individual processes will be introduced in separate training sessions.

                                       Data transfer
                                       Your order data will be passed on for further processing to A+W Production for
                                       production or to A+W Standard Optimizer to cutting optimization. This only
                                       works if the product and article numbers in A+W Business and
                                       A+W Production have been allocated. For other programs, you can define an
                                       appropriate allocation key in Product management > Production tab in field
                                       Optimization key.
                                       For the production of toughened glass, laminated glass, cast resin, etc., the
                                       product will be broken down to bill of material level for A+W Production. The
                                       production start is reported to A+W Business on unit level. Depending on the
                                       setting, the order status can be raised now. These settings will be introduced
                                       in the session on Reports.
                                        “Reports from Production” on page E-56
                                       Orders can be transferred in different ways, no matter whether capacities are
                                       scheduled first:
                                       •   Manual transfer to Production
                                           Manual transfer of orders is done by means of the Transfer to Production
                                           dialog, where you can transfer all orders of a Number Manager with a sta-
                                           tus that is equal to or higher than the Production release status and lower
                                           than the status scheduled in detail.
                                       •   Automatic transfer to Production via workflow task
                                           A workflow task with an appropriate interval is defined for automatic trans-
                                           fer so that the program will regularly search for orders to be transferred to
                                           Capacity Planning or Production. This workflow task will be explained in a
5.20 / 04-2020




                                           separate chapter.
                                            “Transfer to Production via Workflow Task” on page E-24




                 A+W Business Production                                                                          E-19
                 Transfer to Production                                                                             Tutorial




                                          OrderXML
                                          The OrderXML format is based on the standardized OpenTrans interface, with
                                          specific extensions for production-relevant data such as glass, Georgian bars,
                                          or processing.
                                          The production software recognizes the format as that of an order. A separate
                                          file will be created for every order that is transferred to Production. The loca-
                                          tion for the transfer file must be defined in A+W Business and
                                          A+W Production.

                                          Status check
                                          Status points have to be completely defined and allocated for both manual and
                                          automatic transfer to Production. The system uses these status allocations for
                                          checking whether the order data can be transferred.
                                          The allocations were adapted to your business and implemented before the
                                          installation of A+W Business. The basics on status points and allocations have
                                          already been introduced in the training sessions on master data and sales.
                                          This is why we are not going to spend any more time on this subject here.

                                          Cancellation
                                          Every order can be canceled up to a certain point. This point must be defined
                                          internally.
                                          When transfer to Production is canceled, the transferred order will be trans-
                                          ferred to Production again. A cancellation code is set which tells the user on
                                          the shop floor that this order has been canceled.

                                          Special case: optimization of quotations
                                          Quotations can be transferred to Production just to calculate the cutting yield.
                                          This function is available if one of the following versions of transfer to Produc-
                                          tion is used:
                                          •   No capacity planning
                                          •   A+W Business Capacity Planning
                                          The function is blocked if transfer to Production is activated by offers via work-
                                          flow task.
                                          The transfer of quotations for optimization purposes is explained in detail in a
                                          separate training session.
                                           “Transfer to Quotation Optimization” on page E-50
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-20                                                                           A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                       Transfer to Production

                                       nized quite differently in your company.

                 A+W Business Production                                                                          E-23
                 Transfer to Production                                                                           Tutorial




                                          Changing transferred Items
                                          When an order that has been transferred to production, its status is 40. If such
                                          an order is changed, there are two possible scenarios:
                                          •   Changes in prices, discounts, etc. which are irrelevant for production will
                                              not change the status, nor does the order have to be transferred again.
                                          •   When quantities, sizes, glass types, or similar details are changed, the or-
                                              der gets a special code and is immediately transferred to Production by
                                              means of a workflow task.
                                          Company organization must define what is going to happen with items that
                                          have already been produced. You can, for example, define that an order item
                                          has to be canceled and created again.


                                          Transfer of Orders with Purchase Orders
                                          If you produce IG with toughened lites, for example, but do not manufacture
                                          the toughened sheets yourself, the production process depends on the deliv-
                                          ery of the toughened sheets. After booking the receipt of goods, data can be
                                          automatically transferred to A+W Production. If the goods received include
                                          such toughened lites, the start of production is triggered for the corresponding
                                          IG units.
                                          Automatic transfer of goods received is linked with the receipt of goods in Pur-
                                          chasing.


                                          Transfer to Production via Workflow Task
                                          A workflow task serves to process orders automatically whenever possible. If
                                          and to what extent manual intervention is required between two consecutive
                                          workflow tasks depends on the organization of processes in your company.
                                          The necessary settings are defined at installation and should not be changed
                                          afterwards. This chapter therefore only deals with the schematic processes.
                                          Every workflow task consists of one or more customizing formulas. In these
                                          formulas, the individual actions are defined that should be performed. A+W
                                          Business Interface Service (AIS) executes the tasks either periodically or at a
                                          fixed time.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-24                                                                         A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                    Transfer to Production




                                       Settings for the workflow task
                                       Three steps are necessary for defining a workflow task:
                                       •   Enter the formula for automatic transfer to Production in Master Data >
                                           Company > Formulas.
                                       •   Allocate the formula to a workflow task in Master Data > Company > Cus-
                                           tomizing > Workflow tasks tab.
                                       •   Set the workflow task in Master Data > Company > Customizing > Autom.
                                           process execution tab.
                                       Please ask a member of the A+W Software GmbH service team for support
                                       when you change the transfer to Production to workflow task.
                                       This section shows the settings using an example which may differ from the
                                       settings at your company.


                                        How to check the settings for the workflow task
                                       1 Go to the Master Data menu> Company > Customizing then proceed to
                                         the Workflow tasks tab.




                                           Fig. E-3    Example: Workflow tasks


                                           This tab shows the workflow tasks defined for A+W Business and the allo-
                                           cated formulas.
                                       2 Select the workflow task you want to edit.
                                       3 Go to the tab Autom. process execution.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 A+W Business Production                                                                     E-25
                 Transfer to Production                                                                              Tutorial




                                                                                            A        B




                                             A Starting time or interval, depending   B Time or interval
                                               on the execution type
                                             Fig. E-4      Process execution for workflow tasks


                                             This tab defines the starting times and intervals for the defined workflow
                                             tasks. The Execution column offers a selection of valid settings when you
                                             click on a field.
                                          4 Change the starting time and interval if required:
                                             •   If the data are to be transferred periodically, choose the time 00:01.
                                             •   If the data are to be transferred at a certain time, enter the time in col-
                                                 umn hh:mm.
                                          5 If several workflow tasks have been defined, the Sequence column shows
                                            the sequence in which they are to be run.
                                          6 Go to the menu Start > Save to save the data.
                                             The data will be saved and the workflow task is executed acc. to the new
                                             settings.

                 E-26                                                                             A+W Business Production

                                       Transfer to Production without Capacity
                                       Planning
                                       Objectives

                                       • Introducing the settings for transfer to Production without capacity planning
                                       • Transfer orders to Production
                                       • Canceling the transfer


                                       Benefits

                                       • Transfer order data from A+W Business directly to A+W Production or A+W
                                         Standard Optimizer for production.
                                       • If you produce toughened glass, laminated glass, cast resin, etc., you can transfer
                                         the BOM breakdown without further intervention, thus avoiding data transfer errors.
                                       • If data are transferred automatically via workflow task, the orders are directly
                                         passed on to Production after a defined interval.


                                       Please note:

                                       Transfer orders to           Orders can be transferred to Production either manually
                                       Production                   from a Number Manager or (automatically) via workflow
                                                                    task.

                                       Transfer data                The transfer data are saved in a file which is read by
                                                                    A+W Production. The location of this file must be known
                                                                    to A+W Business and A+W Production.

                                       Transfer of SN files         Transfer of Shaping+Nesting files (SN files) requires the
                                                                    following settings:
                                                                    • Automatic creation must be enabled in company data.
                                                                    • Rules for creating the SN file have to be defined in the
                                                                      Utilities.

                                       Order status                 Status checks before the transfer prevent the orders
                                                                    from being passed on the wrong status.
                                                                    Manual transfer to Production is always made after the
                                                                    minimum and lock status.

                                       Number area                  Orders and quotations must have separate number
                                                                    areas to prevent the documents from changing each
                                                                    other during transfer.

                                       Workflow task                A workflow task has to be defined for automatic transfer
                                                                    to production.
                                                                    The workflow task is entered in the Customizing dialog
                                                                    (per client).

                                       Formula                      The workflow task is defined by a formula.

                                       Data transmission            Automatic transfer to Production transfers order data via
5.20 / 04-2020




                                                                    A+W Business interface service (AIS).




                 A+W Business Production                                                                                 E-27
                 Transfer to Production                                                                         Tutorial




                                          Please note:

                                          Default settings          Company data:
                                                                    • Production tab
                                                                    • Production tab > Orders settings
                                                                    • System tab (for SN files)
                                                                    Master data:
                                                                    • Company > Customizing > Workflow tasks tab

                                             Description of settings
                                             This section describes the general settings and functions for transfer to
                                             Production without capacity planning. The training sessions on transfer to
                                             Production with capacity planning will only point out any differences and
                                             peculiarities.

                                             This is why the training session on Transfer to Production without capacity
                                             planning deserves special attention.

                                       Set up Transfer to Production
                                       The data transfer settings can only be made by a user who has administrator
                                       rights.
                                       This session shows you how to define the parameters for manual transfer to
                                       Production (without capacity planning). The settings will apply to both manual
                                       transfer to Production and for automatic transfer via workflow task.

                                           Changed settings can cause serious errors
                                           The settings for the transfer to Production are usually adapted to the situ-
                                           ation of the company in connection with the installation of A+W Business.
                                           If you change these settings, this will greatly affect the functioning of the
                                           transfer to Production. This can cause serious errors, even to the extent
                                           that order and quotation data cannot be transferred at all.
                                           The description of the settings therefore mainly serves to convey the pro-
                                           cess to you, and enable you to answer questions regarding the settings
                                           quickly should there be the need to contact the service team of A+W Soft-
                                           ware GmbH.

                                       The following instructions exist for this training module:
                                       •   “How to check the settings in company data” on page E-30
                                       •   “How to check the defaults for the transfer to Production” on page E-31

                 E-36                                                                        A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                            Transfer to Production




                                       Cancel Transfer to Production
                                       You can cancel an order after it has been transferred to prevent it from being
                                       produced. To do this, transfer the order again but set a cancellation code.
                                       •   To cancel an order via automatic transfer to Production, set the quantities
                                           of the order items to 0. After that, the order will be transferred to Production
                                           again.

                                           The PPS Webservice for canceling the transfer to Production is loaded au-
                                           tomatically now. The workflow task immediately transfers the order with the
                                           new values.
                                       •   If the status point 810 Transfer AWPool cancelled is allocated to a user sta-
                                           tus, cancelling will set the order status to the desired user status, e.g. by
                                           reducing the status. If status point 810 has not been allocated, the order
                                           maintains its former status.
                                       •   Cancellation is only possible up to P.O. transfer.

                                           Example

                                           An order which was transferred to production has got status 40. Cancellation
                                           will not change the status. When you change the quantity, the order will get a
                                           cancellation code and is therefore immediately transferred by automatic
                                           production transfer through a workflow task.


                                       The following instructions exist for this training module:
                                       •   “How to cancel the transfer to Production manually” on page E-38
                                       •   “How to cancel production in connection with automatic order transfer” on
                                           page E-39
5.20 / 04-2020




                 A+W Business Production                                                                                E-37
                 Transfer to Production                                                                             Tutorial




                                             How to cancel the transfer to Production manually
                                               You can cancel a manually transferred order completely after it has been
                                               transferred to prevent it from being produced. To do this, transfer the order
                                               again manually, but set a cancellation code.
                                            1 Move the order you want to cancel to a new Number Manager.
                                            2 Go to menu Production > Production > Transfer to Production.
                                               The Transfer to Production dialog opens.
                                            3 Select the Number Manager which includes the order.




                 A
                 B

                   cancelled
                 Fig. E-11   Cancel order


                                            4 Select Cancel mode (B).
                                            5 To start the cancellation, go to the menu Start > Execute.
                                               The data are saved with a cancellation code as a file in the defined direc-
                                               tory. The status of the order is changed to Transfer to Production canceled.

                 Tutorial                                                                       Transfer to Production




                                            How to cancel production in connection with automatic order transfer
                                           1 Open the order and go to the Items tab.
                                           2 Select the items you want to cancel.
                                              •   To change the quantity, for example, proceed with step 3.
                                              •   To cancel the whole production, go to menu Edit > Delete and proceed
                                                  with step 5.




                 Fig. E-12   Cancel a transferred item


                                           3 Go to menu Functions > Group item > Change locked item.
                                              Input field Pcs. is released.
                                           4 Enter the new quantity.
                                           5 Go to the menu Start > Save to save the changes.
                                           6 Repeat steps 2 to 5 for all items to be changed.
                                           7 Close item entry and the order.
                                              The workflow task will transfer the amended order to Production automati-
                                              cally.

                                       Transfer to Production by A+W Busi-
                                       ness Capacity Planning
                                       Objectives

                                       • Introducing the settings for transfer to A+W Business Capacity Planning


                                       Benefits

                                       • Order data from A+W Business are automatically transferred to Capacity Planning
                                         first.
                                       • Postponements due to capacity bottlenecks are saved in order after they have
                                         been confirmed by the user.
                                       • If data are transferred automatically via workflow tasks, the orders will be
                                         transferred to Capacity Planning first after a defined interval. After successful
                                         scheduling, they are automatically passed on to Production.


                                       Please note:

                                       Order status                Status checks before the transfer prevent the orders
                                                                   from being passed on with the wrong status.

                                       Number area                 Orders and quotations must have separate number
                                                                   areas to prevent the documents from changing each
                                                                   other during transfer.

                                       Transfer to Capacity        Data are transferred in OrderXML format for capacity
                                       Planning                    planning. ERP Webservice must be installed for this
                                                                   purpose.

                                       Default settings            Company data:
                                                                   • Production tab
                                                                   • Capacity planning tab
                                                                   • Production tab > Orders settings
                                                                   Master data:
                                                                   • Company > Customizing > Workflow tasks tab

                                           Description of settings
                                           The basic settings and functions have been explained in the session on
                                           Transfer to Production without capacity planning. The present session
                                           therefore only deals with differences and additional settings in connection
                                           with the transfer to A+W Business Capacity Planning.

                                       Transfer to Production by A+W Produc-
                                       tion Capacity Planner
                                       Objectives

                                       • Introducing the settings for transfer to A+W Production Capacity Planner


                                       Benefits

                                       • The order data from A+W Business are automatically transferred to A+W
                                         Production Capacity Planner first.
                                       • Postponements due to capacity bottlenecks are saved in order after they have
                                         been confirmed by the user.
                                       • If data are transferred automatically via workflow tasks, the orders will be
                                         transferred to Capacity Planning first after a defined interval. After successful
                                         scheduling, they are automatically passed on to Production.


                                       Please note:

                                       Order status                 Status checks before the transfer prevent the orders
                                                                    from being passed on with the wrong status.

                                       Number area                  The number areas for orders and quotations must be
                                                                    kept separate to prevent quotations from being
                                                                    transferred to A+W Production Capacity Planner.

                                       Transfer to Capacity         Data are transferred in OrderXML format for capacity
                                       Planning                     planning. ERP Webservice must be installed for this
                                                                    purpose.

                                       Default settings             Company data:
                                                                    • Production tab
                                                                    • Capacity planning tab
                                                                    • Production tab > Orders settings
                                                                    Master data:
                                                                    • Company > Customizing > Workflow tasks tab

                                           Description of settings
                                           The basic settings and functions have been explained in the session on
                                           Transfer to Production without capacity planning. The present session
                                           therefore deals only with differences and additional settings in connection
                                           with the transfer to A+W Production Capacity Planner.

                 A+W Business Production                                                                              E-49
                 Transfer to Production                                                                                  Tutorial




                                          Transfer to Quotation Optimization
                                          Objectives

                                          • Transferring quotations to cutting optimization
                                          • Pointing out the differences from transfer to Production


                                          Benefits

                                          • If you have entered rarely used glass types in a quotation, you can transfer the
                                            document to Production for optimization purposes. After calculating the number of
                                            stock plates required and the actual waste, you can check the prices of the
                                            quotation and amend them if necessary.


                                          Please note:

                                          Optimization of quotations   Transferred quotations will not be transferred.

                                          Reports                      You will have to ask the responsible person on the shop
                                                                       floor how many stock plates were actually cut.

                                          Number area                  Orders and quotations must have separate number
                                                                       areas to prevent the documents from changing each
                                                                       other during transfer.

                                          Default settings             Master data:
                                                                       • Order > Number areas
                                                                       Company data:
                                                                       • Production tab
                                                                       • Production tab > Quotation settings

                                             Quotations with active A+W Production Capacity Planner
                                             You can transfer quotations to Production for optimization purposes only if
                                             you do not use capacity planning or are using A+W Business Capacity
                                             Planning. The function is blocked if the transfer to Production is activated
                                             by offers via workflow task.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-50                                                                              A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                        Transfer to Production




                                       Optimization of Quotations
                                       If you have entered rarely used glass types in a quotation, it is essential to
                                       make sure that the sales price is calculated so as to avoid losses. You can
                                       transfer the quotation to Production in order to plan the cutting process and
                                       thus determine the glass required as well as the waste.
                                       Quotations with a quotation code will be transferred to Production. The items
                                       of the quotation will not be produced.
                                       There will be no feedback on quotations. After optimization, you will have to
                                       ask the person in charge on the shop floor how many stock plates were actu-
                                       ally cut. This information will help you to calculate the sales price for your quo-
                                       tation or for the ensuing order.

                                           Transfer via workflow task
                                           The offers are generally transfered through an own workflow task. This
                                           form of transfer does not differ from the transfer of the orders.

                                            “Transfer to Production via Workflow Task” on page E-24
5.20 / 04-2020

                 Transfer to Production                                                                              Tutorial




                                          Set up Transfer of Quotations
                                          Transfer of quotations to optimization is set up in the same way as the transfer

                                          the transfer of orders to Production.
                                          In case of OrderXML transer you can define the transfer of quotations in the
                                          same way as for orders. The transfer includes a code that helps to distinguish
                                          quotations and orders.

                                             General settings
                                             Most of the settings for the optimization of quotations are the same as for
                                             the transfer of orders. This instruction only describes the settings which ap-
                                             ply to quotations.

                                              “How to check the defaults for the transfer to Production” on page E-31

                 A+W Business Production                                                                           E-55
                 Reports from Production                                                                           Tutorial




                                           Reports from Production
                                           This chapter introduces the reports from Production. You will learn how to set
                                           up A+W Business so that you can receive these reports.
                                           This includes the following training modules:
                                           •   “Production Reports via Files” on page E-57
                                           •   “File-less Production Report” on page E-68
                                           •   “A+W Business Interface Service” on page E-77

                                           Production reports
                                           Production reports in A+W Business serve to provide information on the pro-
                                           duction progress. The reports update the status of items and orders.
                                           Reports can be created and read in the following ways:
                                           •   Report file:
                                               Report files are created by A+W Production and imported by the
                                               A+W Business Interface Service (AIS). This program runs centrally on the
                                               server and checks the defined directories periodically for new items.
                                           •   File-less report:
                                               A+W Business loads the data online from A+W Production. This online
                                               query is precise with regard to time and quantities and reflects the exact
                                               state of production of an order.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-56                                                                          A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                          Reports from Production




                                       Production Reports via Files
                                       Objectives

                                       •   Introducing report files
                                       •   Basic understanding of shop floor data collection
                                       •   Defining registration points for production reports from A+W Production
                                       •   Defining the transfer paths for the report files


                                       Benefits

                                       • Registration points permit the monitoring of the production progress and thus
                                         check the actual state of an order or of order items.
                                       • Overviews of the status of items and orders can be displayed by registration point.
                                       • Shipping papers can be printed without delay.


                                       Please note:

                                       Registration point           A registration point (RP) is a place on the shop floor
                                                                    where a production step is registered, e.g. the cutting of
                                                                    the first lite of an order.
                                                                    In A+W Business, a status point is allocated to the RP so
                                                                    that the status of an order will be changed by the report
                                                                    from the corresponding RP.

                                       Shop floor data collection   Shop floor data collection in A+W Production monitors
                                                                    the production of every single order on the shop floor.

                                       Report from                  Report files from A+W Production are moved to a server
                                       A+W Production               and are analyzed by A+W Business.

                                       File import interval         The report files are imported by the A+W Business
                                                                    Interface Service (AIS). You can define the interval.

                                       Default settings             Master data:
                                                                    • Registration points - Production
                                                                    • Interface service
                                                                    Company data:
                                                                    • Stock/PP/EDI tab
                                                                    • Production tab
5.20 / 04-2020




                 A+W Business Production                                                                                 E-57
                 Reports from Production                                                                                        Tutorial




                                           Report Files
                                           In A+W Production, data are collected from all vital registration points (RP) on
                                           the shop floor, and are passed on as report files. These production reports
                                           serve for monitoring the production progress in A+W Business. This allows
                                           you to check the actual status of an order.
                                           These files can be sent in two different formats:
                                           •   STS*.ASC files from registration points
                                           •   AWB_STAT files from shop floor data collection
                                           In addition to the registration points in A+W Business, more registration points
                                           can be agreed and defined in A+W Production, e.g. machine allocations.
                                           These are usually reported by STSD file to A+W Business. The code for these
                                           registration points must be higher than 200 so that it can be processed prop-
                                           erly.


                 A+W Production            Report from                     Action in A+W Business
                 file

                 STSP                      Production                      Reports are made mainly by piece. You can define in
                                           e.g. A+W Production RP          A+W Business whether the status should be raised
                                           600, 700, 800 and 900           with the first sheet or only after reports on all lites of
                                                                           an order have been made.

                 STSL                      Planning                        When a new order number has been loaded in
                                           e.g. RP 0, 100, 150 and 200     A+W Production, the order is set in A+W Business to
                                                                           the status allocated to the registration point in
                                                                           A+W Business.
                                                                           If registration point 0 is reported, the status is reset to
                                                                           the value defined in status management.
                                                                           If a registration point is listed to which no status has
                                                                           been assigned, the status will be processed and
                                                                           changed in time management.

                 STSD                      Barcoding                       Barcode reports in A+W Business serve to update
                                           e.g. for machines               the order status, the production date, and the main or
                                                                           item number.
                                                                           Reports are made mainly by piece. You can define in
                                                                           A+W Business whether the status shall be raised
                                                                           with the first lite or only after reports on all lites of an
                                                                           order have been made.
                                                                           If a registration point is listed to which no status has
                                                                           been assigned, the status will be processed and
                                                                           changed in time management.

                 STSG                      Rack                            The report from registration point 900 means that the
                                           RP 900                          rack has been booked as 'shipped' on the defined
                                                                           date.

                 Tab. E-1    Examples of report files from registration points (Section 1 of 2)

                                          If STSP, STSL, STSD, STSB, STSG are being used, a registration point as-
                                          signed to a status point must be selected in company data. If no such registra-
                                          tion point has been assigned, the report will cause an error.
                                          Reports from detailed scheduling and from produced units are saved in
                                          A+W Business in separate database tables with the corresponding fields, e.g.
                                          by order, item, and BOM ID.
                                          Completed items are registered via A+W Production barcodes. This informa-
                                          tion is passed on as a report to A+W Business, which results in the raising of
                                          the A+W Business item status.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 A+W Business Production                                                                                     E-59
                 Reports from Production                                                                           Tutorial




                                           Registration Points for Reports from Production
                                           Registration points (RP) in A+W Production monitor the state of production
                                           and send reports to A+W Business. The files are imported by A+W Business
                                           Interface Service.
                                           In A+W Business, each registration point is allocated to a status point so that
                                           the reports change the status of the item or of the order depending on the reg-
                                           istration point.
                                           Production reports are expected by default from the following registration
                                           points:

                                              Registration point      Meaning
                                              = A+W Production status

                                              0                         unscheduled

                                              100                       scheduled in batch

                                              150                       detailed scheduling

                                              200                       released for production

                                              300                       being produced

                                              350                       breakage on the shop floor

                                              700                       produced

                                              800                       ready for shipment

                                              900                       delivered


                                           This way, A+W Business can give you an overview of the state of the produced
                                           items or orders. The information from the reports show at least the item status
                                           per item, the quantity produced, and the date. Other data are reported depend-
                                           ing on the file type.
                                           For orders or partial orders which have been reported complete and which are
                                           ready to be shipped, printing of shipping papers can be triggered without de-
                                           lay.
5.20 / 04-2020




                 E-60                                                                             A+W Business Production
                 Tutorial                                                                          Reports from Production




                                            Registration Point Allocation
                                            To analyze the reports from A+W Production in A+W Business, you have to al-
                                            locate a status point to every registration point, and adapt the corresponding
                                            data in the interface service. These allocations are needed for production re-
                                            ports and barcode reports.
                                            This session shows you how to allocate a status point for reports from a reg-
                                            istration point in A+W Production. The next training session will tell you how to
                                            set up the interfaces.


                                             How to allocate a registration point for the report per file
                                            1 Go to menu Master data > Production > Registration points production.
                                                The dialog of that name opens.
                                            2 Go to the menu Start > New to switch to the input mode.

                                           3 Enter the name (A) of the A+W Production registration point.
                                              Enter a registration point that can be used to report an order shipped, for
                                              example.
                                           4 Choose the status point (B) and the type (D).

                 A+W Business Production                                                                                E-67
                 Reports from Production                                                                                  Tutorial




                                           File-less Production Report
                                           Objectives

                                           • Defining the transmission route for file-less reports from A+W Production


                                           Benefits

                                           • An order's exact production progress is loaded online from A+W Production and
                                             displayed in the dialog Status report overview.
                                           • The online query helps to avoid malfunctions (missing bookings, double bookings)
                                             as far as possible so that differences in the production progress between
                                             A+W Production and the view in A+W Business cannot occur.


                                           Please note:

                                           Registration point          Even for file-less reports, registration points have to be
                                                                       allocated in the master data in A+W Business.
                                                                       All necessary registration points have to be defined with
                                                                       type 1-Other.

                                           Online report from          Reports are imported by A+W Production via ERP web
                                           A+W Production              service and are booked by A+W Business Interface
                                                                       Service.

                                           Default settings            Master data:
                                                                       • Registration points - Production
                                                                       Company data:
                                                                       • Stock/PP/EDI tab
                                                                       • Production tab
                                                                       In A+W Production, the CommonBase switch Use
                                                                       WebService instead of STS*.ASC must be active.

                 E-68                                                                              A+W Business Production
